# Formatting of some strings

STR_FORMAT_DATE_LONG                                            :{STRING} {STRING} {NUM}

STR_FORMAT_GROUP_NAME                                           :Hópur {COMMA}
STR_FORMAT_INDUSTRY_NAME                                        :{TOWN} {STRING}
